"File Description:   
*List of the device offset percentages and device offset amounts for all HCPCS code with CY 2023 claims data.

*The final CY 2025 portion of the APC payment amounts uniquely associated with the cost of devices.  The device offset percentage for each HCPCS code is used to evaluate whether the procedure is designated as device-intensive, which is required to have device offset greater than 30 percent, and meet other criteria.  

*The applicable device offset amount is the product of the APC payment rate multiplied by HCPCS device offset percent.

*Device cost statistics reflect the data from CY 2023 used for ratesetting in this CY 2025 OPPS/ASC final rule with comment period. Device cost statistics for HCPCS codes established in CY 2024 or CY 2025 do not appear in this file."
